> **PUMP & DUMP ANALÄ°Z Bu program, kripto para**

> **PUMP & DUMP ANALÄ°Z Bu program, kripto para borsalarÄ± ve kripto ile ilgili web sayfalarÄ±ndan, farklÄ± yÃ¶ntemlerle (18 farklÄ± veri toplama yÃ¶ntemi) veri toplayarak, dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼k hacimli coinleri tespit etmek iÃ§in yapÄ±lacaktÄ±r. Web Scraping (Web KazÄ±ma) NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? BorsanÄ±n web sitesinde canlÄ± olarak yayÄ±nlanan verileri HTML Ã¼zerinden alÄ±rsÄ±n. Gerekenler: â€¢ Python: requests, BeautifulSoup â€¢ Dinamik sayfalar iÃ§in: Selenium, undetected-chromedriver â€¢ Proxy havuzu / rotasyon aracÄ± AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ API gerektirmez â€¢ HTML Ã¼zerinden her tÃ¼rlÃ¼ veri Ã§ekilebilir DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Site yapÄ±sÄ± deÄŸiÅŸirse kod kÄ±rÄ±labilir â€¢ IP engeli, CAPTCHA riskleri Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from selenium import webdriver import random, time proxies = load_proxy_list() # Proxy listesini yÃ¼kleyen fonksiyon proxy = random.choice(proxies) options = webdriver.ChromeOptions() options.add_argument('--headless') options.add_argument(f'--proxy-server={proxy}') driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options) driver.get('https://exchange.com/markets') time.sleep(2) soup = BeautifulSoup(driver.page_source, 'html.parser') driver.quit() for row in soup.select('.market-row'): symbol = row.select_one('.symbol').text volume = float(row.select_one('.volume').text.replace(',','')) if volume < 1000: print(symbol, volume) ________________________________________ 2. WebSocket BaÄŸlantÄ±larÄ±nÄ± Analiz Etmek NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? WebSocket streamâ€™lerine baÄŸlanÄ±p JSON mesajlarÄ±nÄ± parse ederek canlÄ± verileri alÄ±rsÄ±n. Gerekenler: â€¢ Python: websockets, asyncio AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ GerÃ§ek zamanlÄ±, dÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼k gecikme DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Protokol deÄŸiÅŸimlerine duyarlÄ± Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import asyncio, websockets, json async def stream(): uri = 'wss://stream.binance.com:9443/ws/!miniTicker@arr' async with websockets.connect(uri) as ws: while True: data = json.loads(await ws.recv()) for t in data: if float(t['Q']) < 1000: print(t['s'], t['Q']) asyncio.run(stream()) ________________________________________ 3. RSS/JSON Endpointâ€™leri NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? BorsanÄ±n saÄŸladÄ±ÄŸÄ± JSON/XML feedâ€™leri HTTP GET ile Ã§ekersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ Python: requests, xml.etree veya json AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ YapÄ±landÄ±rÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸ, kolay Ã§ekim DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Limitler olabilir Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import requests resp = requests.get('https://api.exchange.com/markets.json', timeout=5) coins = resp.json()['data'] low = [c for c in coins if c['volume24h'] < 500] print([c['symbol'] for c in low]) ________________________________________ 4. TarayÄ±cÄ± Otomasyonu (Selenium) NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? Dinamik yÃ¼klenen sayfalarda Selenium ile DOM etkileÅŸimi saÄŸlarsÄ±n. Gerekenler: â€¢ selenium, undetected-chromedriver AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ JavaScript ile yÃ¼klenen her veri alÄ±nabilir DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ YavaÅŸ, kaynak kullanÄ±mÄ± yÃ¼ksek Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: from selenium import webdriver from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By from selenium.webdriver.support.ui import WebDriverWait from selenium.webdriver.support import expected_conditions as EC driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=webdriver.ChromeOptions().add_argument('--headless')) driver.get('https://dynamic.exchange.com') rows = WebDriverWait(driver,10).until( EC.presence_of_all_elements_located((By.CSS_SELECTOR, '.row')) ) for r in rows: print([c.text for c in r.find_elements(By.TAG_NAME,'td')]) driver.quit() ________________________________________ 5. API Proxy / Gateway KullanÄ±mÄ± NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? ÃœÃ§Ã¼ncÃ¼ taraf hizmetlerden (Nomics, CryptoCompare) REST API ile verileri Ã§ekersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ Abonelik / API key AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Tek bir endpointâ€™ten Ã§oklu borsaya eriÅŸim DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Ãœcretli, kotalÄ± olabilir Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import requests url='https://api.nomics.com/v1/currencies/ticker' params={'key':API_KEY,'interval':'1d'} coins=requests.get(url,params=params).json() print([c['currency'] for c in coins if float(c['1d']['volume'])<1000]) ________________________________________ 6. Makine Ã–ÄŸrenimi & Analitik NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? Toplanan Ã¶zelliklerle (volume, volatility) ML modeli kurarsÄ±n. Gerekenler: â€¢ scikit-learn, pandas AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Otomatik pattern tespiti DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Model bakÄ±mÄ± ve veri kalitesi yÃ¼kÃ¼ Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: from sklearn.cluster import DBSCAN X=df[['volume','volatility']] model=DBSCAN(eps=0.5).fit(X) df['lbl']=model.labels_ print(df[df['lbl']==-1]) ________________________________________ 8. Hacim Anomalisi Tespiti NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? Prophet/ARIMA modelleriyle sapmalarÄ± iÅŸaretlersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ prophet veya statsmodels AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Ä°statistiksel gÃ¼venilirlik DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ EÄŸitim sÃ¼resi, parametre ayarÄ± Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: from prophet import Prophet df2=pd.DataFrame({'ds':dates,'y':volumes}) model=Prophet().fit(df2) forecast=model.predict(df2) print(forecast[abs(forecast['yhat']-df2['y'])>threshold]) ________________________________________ 10. Robots.txt KontrolÃ¼ NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? robots.txt ile izinli endpointâ€™leri belirlersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ urllib.robotparser AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Yasal uyumluluk DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ GÃ¼ncel olmayabilir Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import urllib.robotparser rp=urllib.robotparser.RobotFileParser() rp.set_url('https://exchange.com/robots.txt'); rp.read() print(rp.can_fetch('*','https://exchange.com/markets')) ________________________________________ 11. DEX / The Graph SorgularÄ± NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? GraphQL ile subgraphâ€™lardan veri Ã§ekersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ GraphQL client AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ On chain likidite & hacim verisi DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Ä°ndeksleme gecikmeleri Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: from gql import Client,gql from gql.transport.requests import RequestsHTTPTransport client=Client(transport=RequestsHTTPTransport(url=URL)) query=gql('{tokens(first:10,orderBy:volumeUSD){symbol,volumeUSD}}') print(client.execute(query)) ________________________________________ 12. Ã–zel Proxy / VPN KullanÄ±mÄ± NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? Proxy veya VPN ile IP engelini aÅŸarsÄ±n. Gerekenler: â€¢ Proxy listesi/VPN AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ IP engeli sorununu Ã§Ã¶zer DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Maliyet, baÄŸlantÄ± hÄ±zÄ± azalabilir Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import requests proxies={'http':'http://u:p@host:port'} r=requests.get('https://exchange.com',proxies=proxies) print(r.status_code) ________________________________________ 13. Bulk Data Dumps (Flat Files) NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? CSV/JSON arÅŸiv dosyalarÄ±nÄ± indirip iÅŸlersin. Gerekenler: â€¢ SaÄŸlayÄ±cÄ± aboneliÄŸi, depolama AvantajlarÄ±: â€¢ Backtest & analiz iÃ§in bÃ¼yÃ¼k set DezavantajlarÄ±: â€¢ GerÃ§ek zamanlÄ± deÄŸil Ä°leri DÃ¼zey Kodlama Ã–rneÄŸi: import gzip, json with gzip.open('data.json.gz','rt') as f: for ln in f: rec=json.loads(ln) if rec['volume']<1000: process(rec) ________________________________________ 14. Mempool Ä°zleme (eth_subscribe) NasÄ±l Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r? JSON RPC WebSocket Ã¼zerinden yeni pending transactionâ€™larÄ± dinlersin.
